Chapter 1

[1 NIV] The LORD spoke to Moses in the Tent of Meeting in the Desert of Sinai on the first day of the second month of the second year after the Israelites came out of Egypt. He said:
[1 KJV] And the LORD spake unto Moses in the wilderness of Sinai, in the tabernacle of the congregation, on the first day of the second month, in the second year after they were come out of the land of Egypt, saying,
[2 NIV] "Take a census of the whole Israelite community by their clans and families, listing every man by name, one by one.
[2 KJV] Take ye the sum of all the congregation of the children of Israel, after their families, by the house of their fathers, with the number of their names, every male by their polls;
[3 NIV] You and Aaron are to number by their divisions all the men in Israel twenty years old or more who are able to serve in the army.
[3 KJV] From twenty years old and upward, all that are able to go forth to war in Israel: thou and Aaron shall number them by their armies.
[4 NIV] One man from each tribe, each the head of his family, is to help you.
[4 KJV] And with you there shall be a man of every tribe; every one head of the house of his fathers.
[5 NIV] These are the names of the men who are to assist you: from Reuben, Elizur son of Shedeur;
[5 KJV] And these are the names of the men that shall stand with you: of the tribe of Reuben; Elizur the son of Shedeur.
[6 NIV] from Simeon, Shelumiel son of Zurishaddai;
[6 KJV] Of Simeon; Shelumiel the son of Zurishaddai.
[7 NIV] from Judah, Nahshon son of Amminadab;
[7 KJV] Of Judah; Nahshon the son of Amminadab.
[8 NIV] from Issachar, Nethanel son of Zuar;
[8 KJV] Of Issachar; Nethaneel the son of Zuar.
[9 NIV] from Zebulun, Eliab son of Helon;
[9 KJV] Of Zebulun; Eliab the son of Helon.
[10 NIV] from the sons of Joseph: from Ephraim, Elishama son of Ammihud; from Manasseh, Gamaliel son of Pedahzur;
[10 KJV] Of the children of Joseph: of Ephraim; Elishama the son of Ammihud: of Manasseh; Gamaliel the son of Pedahzur.
[11 NIV] from Benjamin, Abidan son of Gideoni;
[11 KJV] Of Benjamin; Abidan the son of Gideoni.
[12 NIV] from Dan, Ahiezer son of Ammishaddai;
[12 KJV] Of Dan; Ahiezer the son of Ammishaddai.
[13 NIV] from Asher, Pagiel son of Ocran;
[13 KJV] Of Asher; Pagiel the son of Ocran.
[14 NIV] from Gad, Eliasaph son of Deuel;
[14 KJV] Of Gad; Eliasaph the son of Deuel.
[15 NIV] from Naphtali, Ahira son of Enan."
[15 KJV] Of Naphtali; Ahira the son of Enan.
[16 NIV] These were the men appointed from the community, the leaders of their ancestral tribes. They were the heads of the clans of Israel.
[16 KJV] These were the renowned of the congregation, princes of the tribes of their fathers, heads of thousands in Israel.
[17 NIV] Moses and Aaron took these men whose names had been given,
[17 KJV] And Moses and Aaron took these men which are expressed by their names:
[18 NIV] and they called the whole community together on the first day of the second month. The people indicated their ancestry by their clans and families, and the men twenty years old or more were listed by name, one by one,
[18 KJV] And they assembled all the congregation together on the first day of the second month, and they declared their pedigrees after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, by their polls.
[19 NIV] as the LORD commanded Moses. And so he counted them in the Desert of Sinai:
[19 KJV] As the LORD commanded Moses, so he numbered them in the wilderness of Sinai.
[20 NIV] From the descendants of Reuben the firstborn son of Israel: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, one by one, according to the records of their clans and families.
[20 KJV] And the children of Reuben, Israel's eldest son, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, by their polls, every male from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[21 NIV] The number from the tribe of Reuben was 46,500.
[21 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Reuben, were forty and six thousand and five hundred.
[22 NIV] From the descendants of Simeon: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were counted and listed by name, one by one, according to the records of their clans and families.
[22 KJV] Of the children of Simeon, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, those that were numbered of them, according to the number of the names, by their polls, every male from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[23 NIV] The number from the tribe of Simeon was 59,300.
[23 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Simeon, were fifty and nine thousand and three hundred.
[24 NIV] From the descendants of Gad: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[24 KJV] Of the children of Gad, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[25 NIV] The number from the tribe of Gad was 45,650.
[25 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Gad, were forty and five thousand six hundred and fifty.
[26 NIV] From the descendants of Judah: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[26 KJV] Of the children of Judah, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[27 NIV] The number from the tribe of Judah was 74,600.
[27 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Judah, were threescore and fourteen thousand and six hundred.
[28 NIV] From the descendants of Issachar: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[28 KJV] Of the children of Issachar, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[29 NIV] The number from the tribe of Issachar was 54,400.
[29 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Issachar, were fifty and four thousand and four hundred.
[30 NIV] From the descendants of Zebulun: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[30 KJV] Of the children of Zebulun, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[31 NIV] The number from the tribe of Zebulun was 57,400.
[31 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Zebulun, were fifty and seven thousand and four hundred.
[32 NIV] From the sons of Joseph: From the descendants of Ephraim: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[32 KJV] Of the children of Joseph, namely, of the children of Ephraim, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[33 NIV] The number from the tribe of Ephraim was 40,500.
[33 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Ephraim, were forty thousand and five hundred.
[34 NIV] From the descendants of Manasseh: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[34 KJV] Of the children of Manasseh, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[35 NIV] The number from the tribe of Manasseh was 32,200.
[35 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Manasseh, were thirty and two thousand and two hundred.
[36 NIV] From the descendants of Benjamin: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[36 KJV] Of the children of Benjamin, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[37 NIV] The number from the tribe of Benjamin was 35,400.
[37 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Benjamin, were thirty and five thousand and four hundred.
[38 NIV] From the descendants of Dan: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[38 KJV] Of the children of Dan, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[39 NIV] The number from the tribe of Dan was 62,700.
[39 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Dan, were threescore and two thousand and seven hundred.
[40 NIV] From the descendants of Asher: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[40 KJV] Of the children of Asher, by their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[41 NIV] The number from the tribe of Asher was 41,500.
[41 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Asher, were forty and one thousand and five hundred.
[42 NIV] From the descendants of Naphtali: All the men twenty years old or more who were able to serve in the army were listed by name, according to the records of their clans and families.
[42 KJV] Of the children of Naphtali, throughout their generations, after their families, by the house of their fathers, according to the number of the names, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war;
[43 NIV] The number from the tribe of Naphtali was 53,400.
[43 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, even of the tribe of Naphtali, were fifty and three thousand and four hundred.
[44 NIV] These were the men counted by Moses and Aaron and the twelve leaders of Israel, each one representing his family.
[44 KJV] These are those that were numbered, which Moses and Aaron numbered, and the princes of Israel, being twelve men: each one was for the house of his fathers.
[45 NIV] All the Israelites twenty years old or more who were able to serve in Israel's army were counted according to their families.
[45 KJV] So were all those that were numbered of the children of Israel, by the house of their fathers, from twenty years old and upward, all that were able to go forth to war in Israel;
[46 NIV] The total number was 603,550.
[46 KJV] Even all they that were numbered were six hundred thousand and three thousand and five hundred and fifty.
[47 NIV] The families of the tribe of Levi, however, were not counted along with the others.
[47 KJV] But the Levites after the tribe of their fathers were not numbered among them.
[48 NIV] The LORD had said to Moses:
[48 KJV] For the LORD had spoken unto Moses, saying,
[49 NIV] "You must not count the tribe of Levi or include them in the census of the other Israelites.
[49 KJV] Only thou shalt not number the tribe of Levi, neither take the sum of them among the children of Israel:
[50 NIV] Instead, appoint the Levites to be in charge of the tabernacle of the Testimony--over all its furnishings and everything belonging to it. They are to carry the tabernacle and all its furnishings; they are to take care of it and encamp around it.
[50 KJV] But thou shalt appoint the Levites over the tabernacle of testimony, and over all the vessels thereof, and over all things that belong to it: they shall bear the tabernacle, and all the vessels thereof; and they shall minister unto it, and shall encamp round about the tabernacle.
[51 NIV] Whenever the tabernacle is to move, the Levites are to take it down, and whenever the tabernacle is to be set up, the Levites shall do it. Anyone else who goes near it shall be put to death.
[51 KJV] And when the tabernacle setteth forward, the Levites shall take it down: and when the tabernacle is to be pitched, the Levites shall set it up: and the stranger that cometh nigh shall be put to death.
[52 NIV] The Israelites are to set up their tents by divisions, each man in his own camp under his own standard.
[52 KJV] And the children of Israel shall pitch their tents, every man by his own camp, and every man by his own standard, throughout their hosts.
[53 NIV] The Levites, however, are to set up their tents around the tabernacle of the Testimony so that wrath will not fall on the Israelite community. The Levites are to be responsible for the care of the tabernacle of the Testimony."
[53 KJV] But the Levites shall pitch round about the tabernacle of testimony, that there be no wrath upon the congregation of the children of Israel: and the Levites shall keep the charge of the tabernacle of testimony.
[54 NIV] The Israelites did all this just as the LORD commanded Moses.
[54 KJV] And the children of Israel did according to all that the LORD commanded Moses, so did they.

Chapter 2

[1 NIV] The LORD said to Moses and Aaron:
[1 KJV] And the LORD spake unto Moses and unto Aaron, saying,
[2 NIV] "The Israelites are to camp around the Tent of Meeting some distance from it, each man under his standard with the banners of his family."
[2 KJV] Every man of the children of Israel shall pitch by his own standard, with the ensign of their father's house: far off about the tabernacle of the congregation shall they pitch.
[3 NIV] On the east, toward the sunrise, the divisions of the camp of Judah are to encamp under their standard. The leader of the people of Judah is Nahshon son of Amminadab.
[3 KJV] And on the east side toward the rising of the sun shall they of the standard of the camp of Judah pitch throughout their armies: and Nahshon the son of Amminadab shall be captain of the children of Judah.
[4 NIV] His division numbers 74,600.
[4 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered of them, were threescore and fourteen thousand and six hundred.
[5 NIV] The tribe of Issachar will camp next to them. The leader of the people of Issachar is Nethanel son of Zuar.
[5 KJV] And those that do pitch next unto him shall be the tribe of Issachar: and Nethaneel the son of Zuar shall be captain of the children of Issachar.
[6 NIV] His division numbers 54,400.
[6 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered thereof, were fifty and four thousand and four hundred.
[7 NIV] The tribe of Zebulun will be next. The leader of the people of Zebulun is Eliab son of Helon.
[7 KJV] Then the tribe of Zebulun: and Eliab the son of Helon shall be captain of the children of Zebulun.
[8 NIV] His division numbers 57,400.
[8 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered thereof, were fifty and seven thousand and four hundred.
[9 NIV] All the men assigned to the camp of Judah, according to their divisions, number 186,400. They will set out first.
[9 KJV] All that were numbered in the camp of Judah were an hundred thousand and fourscore thousand and six thousand and four hundred, throughout their armies. These shall first set forth.
[10 NIV] On the south will be the divisions of the camp of Reuben under their standard. The leader of the people of Reuben is Elizur son of Shedeur.
[10 KJV] On the south side shall be the standard of the camp of Reuben according to their armies: and the captain of the children of Reuben shall be Elizur the son of Shedeur.
[11 NIV] His division numbers 46,500.
[11 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered thereof, were forty and six thousand and five hundred.
[12 NIV] The tribe of Simeon will camp next to them. The leader of the people of Simeon is Shelumiel son of Zurishaddai.
[12 KJV] And those which pitch by him shall be the tribe of Simeon: and the captain of the children of Simeon shall be Shelumiel the son of Zurishaddai.
[13 NIV] His division numbers 59,300.
[13 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered of them, were fifty and nine thousand and three hundred.
[14 NIV] The tribe of Gad will be next. The leader of the people of Gad is Eliasaph son of Deuel. [1]
[14 KJV] Then the tribe of Gad: and the captain of the sons of Gad shall be Eliasaph the son of Reuel.
[15 NIV] His division numbers 45,650.
[15 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered of them, were forty and five thousand and six hundred and fifty.
[16 NIV] All the men assigned to the camp of Reuben, according to their divisions, number 151,450. They will set out second.
[16 KJV] All that were numbered in the camp of Reuben were an hundred thousand and fifty and one thousand and four hundred and fifty, throughout their armies. And they shall set forth in the second rank.
[17 NIV] Then the Tent of Meeting and the camp of the Levites will set out in the middle of the camps. They will set out in the same order as they encamp, each in his own place under his standard.
[17 KJV] Then the tabernacle of the congregation shall set forward with the camp of the Levites in the midst of the camp: as they encamp, so shall they set forward, every man in his place by their standards.
[18 NIV] On the west will be the divisions of the camp of Ephraim under their standard. The leader of the people of Ephraim is Elishama son of Ammihud.
[18 KJV] On the west side shall be the standard of the camp of Ephraim according to their armies: and the captain of the sons of Ephraim shall be Elishama the son of Ammihud.
[19 NIV] His division numbers 40,500.
[19 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered of them, were forty thousand and five hundred.
[20 NIV] The tribe of Manasseh will be next to them. The leader of the people of Manasseh is Gamaliel son of Pedahzur.
[20 KJV] And by him shall be the tribe of Manasseh: and the captain of the children of Manasseh shall be Gamaliel the son of Pedahzur.
[21 NIV] His division numbers 32,200.
[21 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered of them, were thirty and two thousand and two hundred.
[22 NIV] The tribe of Benjamin will be next. The leader of the people of Benjamin is Abidan son of Gideoni.
[22 KJV] Then the tribe of Benjamin: and the captain of the sons of Benjamin shall be Abidan the son of Gideoni.
[23 NIV] His division numbers 35,400.
[23 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered of them, were thirty and five thousand and four hundred.
[24 NIV] All the men assigned to the camp of Ephraim, according to their divisions, number 108,100. They will set out third.
[24 KJV] All that were numbered of the camp of Ephraim were an hundred thousand and eight thousand and an hundred, throughout their armies. And they shall go forward in the third rank.
[25 NIV] On the north will be the divisions of the camp of Dan, under their standard. The leader of the people of Dan is Ahiezer son of Ammishaddai.
[25 KJV] The standard of the camp of Dan shall be on the north side by their armies: and the captain of the children of Dan shall be Ahiezer the son of Ammishaddai.
[26 NIV] His division numbers 62,700.
[26 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered of them, were threescore and two thousand and seven hundred.
[27 NIV] The tribe of Asher will camp next to them. The leader of the people of Asher is Pagiel son of Ocran.
[27 KJV] And those that encamp by him shall be the tribe of Asher: and the captain of the children of Asher shall be Pagiel the son of Ocran.
[28 NIV] His division numbers 41,500.
[28 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered of them, were forty and one thousand and five hundred.
[29 NIV] The tribe of Naphtali will be next. The leader of the people of Naphtali is Ahira son of Enan.
[29 KJV] Then the tribe of Naphtali: and the captain of the children of Naphtali shall be Ahira the son of Enan.
[30 NIV] His division numbers 53,400.
[30 KJV] And his host, and those that were numbered of them, were fifty and three thousand and four hundred.
[31 NIV] All the men assigned to the camp of Dan number 157,600. They will set out last, under their standards.
[31 KJV] All they that were numbered in the camp of Dan were an hundred thousand and fifty and seven thousand and six hundred. They shall go hindmost with their standards.
[32 NIV] These are the Israelites, counted according to their families. All those in the camps, by their divisions, number 603,550.
[32 KJV] These are those which were numbered of the children of Israel by the house of their fathers: all those that were numbered of the camps throughout their hosts were six hundred thousand and three thousand and five hundred and fifty.
[33 NIV] The Levites, however, were not counted along with the other Israelites, as the LORD commanded Moses.
[33 KJV] But the Levites were not numbered among the children of Israel; as the LORD commanded Moses.
[34 NIV] So the Israelites did everything the LORD commanded Moses; that is the way they encamped under their standards, and that is the way they set out, each with his clan and family.
[34 KJV] And the children of Israel did according to all that the LORD commanded Moses: so they pitched by their standards, and so they set forward, every one after their families, according to the house of their fathers.
1. [14] Many manuscripts of the Masoretic Text, Samaritan Pentateuch and Vulgate (see also Num. 1:14); most manuscripts of the Masoretic Text Reuel

Chapter 3

[1 NIV] This is the account of the family of Aaron and Moses at the time the LORD talked with Moses on Mount Sinai.
[1 KJV] These also are the generations of Aaron and Moses in the day that the LORD spake with Moses in mount Sinai.
[2 NIV] The names of the sons of Aaron were Nadab the firstborn and Abihu, Eleazar and Ithamar.
[2 KJV] And these are the names of the sons of Aaron; Nadab the firstborn, and Abihu, Eleazar, and Ithamar.
[3 NIV] Those were the names of Aaron's sons, the anointed priests, who were ordained to serve as priests.
[3 KJV] These are the names of the sons of Aaron, the priests which were anointed, whom he consecrated to minister in the priest's office.
[4 NIV] Nadab and Abihu, however, fell dead before the LORD when they made an offering with unauthorized fire before him in the Desert of Sinai. They had no sons; so only Eleazar and Ithamar served as priests during the lifetime of their father Aaron.
[4 KJV] And Nadab and Abihu died before the LORD, when they offered strange fire before the LORD, in the wilderness of Sinai, and they had no children: and Eleazar and Ithamar ministered in the priest's office in the sight of Aaron their father.
[5 NIV] The LORD said to Moses,
[5 KJV] And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
[6 NIV] "Bring the tribe of Levi and present them to Aaron the priest to assist him.
[6 KJV] Bring the tribe of Levi near, and present them before Aaron the priest, that they may minister unto him.
[7 NIV] They are to perform duties for him and for the whole community at the Tent of Meeting by doing the work of the tabernacle.
[7 KJV] And they shall keep his charge, and the charge of the whole congregation before the tabernacle of the congregation, to do the service of the tabernacle.
[8 NIV] They are to take care of all the furnishings of the Tent of Meeting, fulfilling the obligations of the Israelites by doing the work of the tabernacle.
[8 KJV] And they shall keep all the instruments of the tabernacle of the congregation, and the charge of the children of Israel, to do the service of the tabernacle.
[9 NIV] Give the Levites to Aaron and his sons; they are the Israelites who are to be given wholly to him. [1]
[9 KJV] And thou shalt give the Levites unto Aaron and to his sons: they are wholly given unto him out of the children of Israel.
[10 NIV] Appoint Aaron and his sons to serve as priests; anyone else who approaches the sanctuary must be put to death."
[10 KJV] And thou shalt appoint Aaron and his sons, and they shall wait on their priest's office: and the stranger that cometh nigh shall be put to death.
[11 NIV] The LORD also said to Moses,
[11 KJV] And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
[12 NIV] "I have taken the Levites from among the Israelites in place of the first male offspring of every Israelite woman. The Levites are mine,
[12 KJV] And I, behold, I have taken the Levites from among the children of Israel instead of all the firstborn that openeth the matrix among the children of Israel: therefore the Levites shall be mine;
[13 NIV] for all the firstborn are mine. When I struck down all the firstborn in Egypt, I set apart for myself every firstborn in Israel, whether man or animal. They are to be mine. I am the LORD."
[13 KJV] Because all the firstborn are mine; for on the day that I smote all the firstborn in the land of Egypt I hallowed unto me all the firstborn in Israel, both man and beast: mine shall they be: I am the LORD.
[14 NIV] The LORD said to Moses in the Desert of Sinai,
[14 KJV] And the LORD spake unto Moses in the wilderness of Sinai, saying,
[15 NIV] "Count the Levites by their families and clans. Count every male a month old or more."
[15 KJV] Number the children of Levi after the house of their fathers, by their families: every male from a month old and upward shalt thou number them.
[16 NIV] So Moses counted them, as he was commanded by the word of the LORD.
[16 KJV] And Moses numbered them according to the word of the LORD, as he was commanded.
[17 NIV] These were the names of the sons of Levi: Gershon, Kohath and Merari.
[17 KJV] And these were the sons of Levi by their names; Gershon, and Kohath, and Merari.
[18 NIV] These were the names of the Gershonite clans: Libni and Shimei.
[18 KJV] And these are the names of the sons of Gershon by their families; Libni, and Shimei.
[19 NIV] The Kohathite clans: Amram, Izhar, Hebron and Uzziel.
[19 KJV] And the sons of Kohath by their families; Amram, and Izehar, Hebron, and Uzziel.
[20 NIV] The Merarite clans: Mahli and Mushi. These were the Levite clans, according to their families.
[20 KJV] And the sons of Merari by their families; Mahli, and Mushi. These are the families of the Levites according to the house of their fathers.
[21 NIV] To Gershon belonged the clans of the Libnites and Shimeites; these were the Gershonite clans.
[21 KJV] Of Gershon was the family of the Libnites, and the family of the Shimites: these are the families of the Gershonites.
[22 NIV] The number of all the males a month old or more who were counted was 7,500.
[22 KJV] Those that were numbered of them, according to the number of all the males, from a month old and upward, even those that were numbered of them were seven thousand and five hundred.
[23 NIV] The Gershonite clans were to camp on the west, behind the tabernacle.
[23 KJV] The families of the Gershonites shall pitch behind the tabernacle westward.
[24 NIV] The leader of the families of the Gershonites was Eliasaph son of Lael.
[24 KJV] And the chief of the house of the father of the Gershonites shall be Eliasaph the son of Lael.
[25 NIV] At the Tent of Meeting the Gershonites were responsible for the care of the tabernacle and tent, its coverings, the curtain at the entrance to the Tent of Meeting,
[25 KJV] And the charge of the sons of Gershon in the tabernacle of the congregation shall be the tabernacle, and the tent, the covering thereof, and the hanging for the door of the tabernacle of the congregation,
[26 NIV] the curtains of the courtyard, the curtain at the entrance to the courtyard surrounding the tabernacle and altar, and the ropes--and everything related to their use.
[26 KJV] And the hangings of the court, and the curtain for the door of the court, which is by the tabernacle, and by the altar round about, and the cords of it for all the service thereof.
[27 NIV] To Kohath belonged the clans of the Amramites, Izharites, Hebronites and Uzzielites; these were the Kohathite clans.
[27 KJV] And of Kohath was the family of the Amramites, and the family of the Izeharites, and the family of the Hebronites, and the family of the Uzzielites: these are the families of the Kohathites.
[28 NIV] The number of all the males a month old or more was 8,600. [2] The Kohathites were responsible for the care of the sanctuary.
[28 KJV] In the number of all the males, from a month old and upward, were eight thousand and six hundred, keeping the charge of the sanctuary.
[29 NIV] The Kohathite clans were to camp on the south side of the tabernacle.

Chapter 5

[1 NIV] The LORD said to Moses,
[1 KJV] And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
[2 NIV] "Command the Israelites to send away from the camp anyone who has an infectious skin disease [1] or a discharge of any kind, or who is ceremonially unclean because of a dead body.
[2 KJV] Command the children of Israel, that they put out of the camp every leper, and every one that hath an issue, and whosoever is defiled by the dead:
[3 NIV] Send away male and female alike; send them outside the camp so they will not defile their camp, where I dwell among them."
[3 KJV] Both male and female shall ye put out, without the camp shall ye put them; that they defile not their camps, in the midst whereof I dwell.
[4 NIV] The Israelites did this; they sent them outside the camp. They did just as the LORD had instructed Moses.
[4 KJV] And the children of Israel did so, and put them out without the camp: as the LORD spake unto Moses, so did the children of Israel.
[5 NIV] The LORD said to Moses,
[5 KJV] And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
[6 NIV] "Say to the Israelites: `When a man or woman wrongs another in any way [2] and so is unfaithful to the LORD, that person is guilty
[6 KJV] Speak unto the children of Israel, When a man or woman shall commit any sin that men commit, to do a trespass against the LORD, and that person be guilty;
[7 NIV] and must confess the sin he has committed. He must make full restitution for his wrong, add one fifth to it and give it all to the person he has wronged.
[7 KJV] Then they shall confess their sin which they have done: and he shall recompense his trespass with the principal thereof, and add unto it the fifth part thereof, and give it unto him against whom he hath trespassed.
[8 NIV] But if that person has no close relative to whom restitution can be made for the wrong, the restitution belongs to the LORD and must be given to the priest, along with the ram with which atonement is made for him.
[8 KJV] But if the man have no kinsman to recompense the trespass unto, let the trespass be recompensed unto the LORD, even to the priest; beside the ram of the atonement, whereby an atonement shall be made for him.
[9 NIV] All the sacred contributions the Israelites bring to a priest will belong to him.
[9 KJV] And every offering of all the holy things of the children of Israel, which they bring unto the priest, shall be his.
[10 NIV] Each man's sacred gifts are his own, but what he gives to the priest will belong to the priest.'"
[10 KJV] And every man's hallowed things shall be his: whatsoever any man giveth the priest, it shall be his.
[11 NIV] Then the LORD said to Moses,
[11 KJV] And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
[12 NIV] "Speak to the Israelites and say to them: `If a man's wife goes astray and is unfaithful to him
[12 KJV] Speak unto the children of Israel, and say unto them, If any man's wife go aside, and commit a trespass against him,
[13 NIV] by sleeping with another man, and this is hidden from her husband and her impurity is undetected (since there is no witness against her and she has not been caught in the act),
[13 KJV] And a man lie with her carnally, and it be hid from the eyes of her husband, and be kept close, and she be defiled, and there be no witness against her, neither she be taken with the manner;
[14 NIV] and if feelings of jealousy come over her husband and he suspects his wife and she is impure--or if he is jealous and suspects her even though she is not impure--
[14 KJV] And the spirit of jealousy come upon him, and he be jealous of his wife, and she be defiled: or if the spirit of jealousy come upon him, and he be jealous of his wife, and she be not defiled:
[15 NIV] then he is to take his wife to the priest. He must also take an offering of a tenth of an ephah [3] of barley flour on her behalf. He must not pour oil on it or put incense on it, because it is a grain offering for jealousy, a reminder offering to draw attention to guilt.
[15 KJV] Then shall the man bring his wife unto the priest, and he shall bring her offering for her, the tenth part of an ephah of barley meal; he shall pour no oil upon it, nor put frankincense thereon; for it is an offering of jealousy, an offering of memorial, bringing iniquity to remembrance.
[16 NIV] "`The priest shall bring her and have her stand before the LORD.
[16 KJV] And the priest shall bring her near, and set her before the LORD:
[17 NIV] Then he shall take some holy water in a clay jar and put some dust from the tabernacle floor into the water.
[17 KJV] And the priest shall take holy water in an earthen vessel; and of the dust that is in the floor of the tabernacle the priest shall take, and put it into the water:
[18 NIV] After the priest has had the woman stand before the LORD, he shall loosen her hair and place in her hands the reminder offering, the grain offering for jealousy, while he himself holds the bitter water that brings a curse.
[18 KJV] And the priest shall set the woman before the LORD, and uncover the woman's head, and put the offering of memorial in her hands, which is the jealousy offering: and the priest shall have in his hand the bitter water that causeth the curse:
[19 NIV] Then the priest shall put the woman under oath and say to her, "If no other man has slept with you and you have not gone astray and become impure while married to your husband, may this bitter water that brings a curse not harm you.
[19 KJV] And the priest shall charge her by an oath, and say unto the woman, If no man have lain with thee, and if thou hast not gone aside to uncleanness with another instead of thy husband, be thou free from this bitter water that causeth the curse:
[20 NIV] But if you have gone astray while married to your husband and you have defiled yourself by sleeping with a man other than your husband"--
[20 KJV] But if thou hast gone aside to another instead of thy husband, and if thou be defiled, and some man have lain with thee beside thine husband:
[21 NIV] here the priest is to put the woman under this curse of the oath--"may the LORD cause your people to curse and denounce you when he causes your thigh to waste away and your abdomen to swell. [4]
[21 KJV] Then the priest shall charge the woman with an oath of cursing, and the priest shall say unto the woman, The LORD make thee a curse and an oath among thy people, when the LORD doth make thy thigh to rot, and thy belly to swell;
[22 NIV] May this water that brings a curse enter your body so that your abdomen swells and your thigh wastes away. [5] " "`Then the woman is to say, "Amen. So be it."
[22 KJV] And this water that causeth the curse shall go into thy bowels, to make thy belly to swell, and thy thigh to rot: And the woman shall say, Amen, amen.
[23 NIV] "`The priest is to write these curses on a scroll and then wash them off into the bitter water.
[23 KJV] And the priest shall write these curses in a book, and he shall blot them out with the bitter water:
[24 NIV] He shall have the woman drink the bitter water that brings a curse, and this water will enter her and cause bitter suffering.
[24 KJV] And he shall cause the woman to drink the bitter water that causeth the curse: and the water that causeth the curse shall enter into her, and become bitter.
[25 NIV] The priest is to take from her hands the grain offering for jealousy, wave it before the LORD and bring it to the altar.
[25 KJV] Then the priest shall take the jealousy offering out of the woman's hand, and shall wave the offering before the LORD, and offer it upon the altar:
[26 NIV] The priest is then to take a handful of the grain offering as a memorial offering and burn it on the altar; after that, he is to have the woman drink the water.
[26 KJV] And the priest shall take an handful of the offering, even the memorial thereof, and burn it upon the altar, and afterward shall cause the woman to drink the water.
[27 NIV] If she has defiled herself and been unfaithful to her husband, then when she is made to drink the water that brings a curse, it will go into her and cause bitter suffering; her abdomen will swell and her thigh waste away, [6] and she will become accursed among her people.
[27 KJV] And when he hath made her to drink the water, then it shall come to pass, that, if she be defiled, and have done trespass against her husband, that the water that causeth the curse shall enter into her, and become bitter, and her belly shall swell, and her thigh shall rot: and the woman shall be a curse among her people.
[28 NIV] If, however, the woman has not defiled herself and is free from impurity, she will be cleared of guilt and will be able to have children.
[28 KJV] And if the woman be not defiled, but be clean; then she shall be free, and shall conceive seed.
[29 NIV] "`This, then, is the law of jealousy when a woman goes astray and defiles herself while married to her husband,
[29 KJV] This is the law of jealousies, when a wife goeth aside to another instead of her husband, and is defiled;
[30 NIV] or when feelings of jealousy come over a man because he suspects his wife. The priest is to have her stand before the LORD and is to apply this entire law to her.
[30 KJV] Or when the spirit of jealousy cometh upon him, and he be jealous over his wife, and shall set the woman before the LORD, and the priest shall execute upon her all this law.
[31 NIV] The husband will be innocent of any wrongdoing, but the woman will bear the consequences of her sin.'"
[31 KJV] Then shall the man be guiltless from iniquity, and this woman shall bear her iniquity.
1. [2] Traditionally leprosy ; the Hebrew word was used for various diseases affecting the skin--not necessarily leprosy.
2. [6] Or woman commits any wrong common to mankind
3. [15] That is, probably about 2 quarts (about 2 liters)
4. [21] Or causes you to have a miscarrying womb and barrenness
5. [22] Or body and cause you to be barren and have a miscarrying womb
6. [27] Or suffering; she will have barrenness and a miscarrying womb

Chapter 6

[1 NIV] The LORD said to Moses,
[1 KJV] And the LORD spake unto Moses, saying,
[2 NIV] "Speak to the Israelites and say to them: `If a man or woman wants to make a special vow, a vow of separation to the LORD as a Nazirite,
[2 KJV] Speak unto the children of Israel, and say unto them, When either man or woman shall separate themselves to vow a vow of a Nazarite, to separate themselves unto the LORD:
[3 NIV] he must abstain from wine and other fermented drink and must not drink vinegar made from wine or from other fermented drink. He must not drink grape juice or eat grapes or raisins.
[3 KJV] He shall separate himself from wine and strong drink, and shall drink no vinegar of wine, or vinegar of strong drink, neither shall he drink any liquor of grapes, nor eat moist grapes, or dried.
[4 NIV] As long as he is a Nazirite, he must not eat anything that comes from the grapevine, not even the seeds or skins.
[4 KJV] All the days of his separation shall he eat nothing that is made of the vine tree, from the kernels even to the husk.
[5 NIV] "`During the entire period of his vow of separation no razor may be used on his head. He must be holy until the period of his separation to the LORD is over; he must let the hair of his head grow long.
[5 KJV] All the days of the vow of his separation there shall no razor come upon his head: until the days be fulfilled, in the which he separateth himself unto the LORD, he shall be holy, and shall let the locks of the hair of his head grow.
[6 NIV] Throughout the period of his separation to the LORD he must not go near a dead body.
[6 KJV] All the days that he separateth himself unto the LORD he shall come at no dead body.
[7 NIV] Even if his own father or mother or brother or sister dies, he must not make himself ceremonially unclean on account of them, because the symbol of his separation to God is on his head.
[7 KJV] He shall not make himself unclean for his father, or for his mother, for his brother, or for his sister, when they die: because the consecration of his God is upon his head.
[8 NIV] Throughout the period of his separation he is consecrated to the LORD.
[8 KJV] All the days of his separation he is holy unto the LORD.
[9 NIV] "`If someone dies suddenly in his presence, thus defiling the hair he has dedicated, he must shave his head on the day of his cleansing--the seventh day.
[9 KJV] And if any man die very suddenly by him, and he hath defiled the head of his consecration; then he shall shave his head in the day of his cleansing, on the seventh day shall he shave it.
[10 NIV] Then on the eighth day he must bring two doves or two young pigeons to the priest at the entrance to the Tent of Meeting.

[11 NIV] The priest is to offer one as a sin offering and the other as a burnt offering to make atonement for him because he sinned by being in the presence of the dead body. That same day he is to consecrate his head.
[11 KJV] And the priest shall offer the one for a sin offering, and the other for a burnt offering, and make an atonement for him, for that he sinned by the dead, and shall hallow his head that same day.
[12 NIV] He must dedicate himself to the LORD for the period of his separation and must bring a year-old male lamb as a guilt offering. The previous days do not count, because he became defiled during his separation.
[12 KJV] And he shall consecrate unto the LORD the days of his separation, and shall bring a lamb of the first year for a trespass offering: but the days that were before shall be lost, because his separation was defiled.
[13 NIV] "`Now this is the law for the Nazirite when the period of his separation is over. He is to be brought to the entrance to the Tent of Meeting.
[13 KJV] And this is the law of the Nazarite, when the days of his separation are fulfilled: he shall be brought unto the door of the tabernacle of the congregation:
[14 NIV] There he is to present his offerings to the LORD: a year-old male lamb without defect for a burnt offering, a year-old ewe lamb without defect for a sin offering, a ram without defect for a fellowship offering, [1]
[14 KJV] And he shall offer his offering unto the LORD, one he lamb of the first year without blemish for a burnt offering, and one ewe lamb of the first year without blemish for a sin offering, and one ram without blemish for peace offerings,
[15 NIV] together with their grain offerings and drink offerings, and a basket of bread made without yeast--cakes made of fine flour mixed with oil, and wafers spread with oil.

[16 NIV] "`The priest is to present them before the LORD and make the sin offering and the burnt offering.

[17 NIV] He is to present the basket of unleavened bread and is to sacrifice the ram as a fellowship offering to the LORD, together with its grain offering and drink offering.
[17 KJV] And he shall offer the ram for a sacrifice of peace offerings unto the LORD, with the basket of unleavened bread: the priest shall offer also his meat offering, and his drink offering.
[18 NIV] "`Then at the entrance to the Tent of Meeting, the Nazirite must shave off the hair that he dedicated. He is to take the hair and put it in the fire that is under the sacrifice of the fellowship offering.
[18 KJV] And the Nazarite shall shave the head of his separation at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, and shall take the hair of the head of his separation, and put it in the fire which is under the sacrifice of the peace offerings.

[20 KJV] And the priest shall wave them for a wave offering before the LORD: this is holy for the priest, with the wave breast and heave shoulder: and after that the Nazarite may drink wine.
[21 NIV] "`This is the law of the Nazirite who vows his offering to the LORD in accordance with his separation, in addition to whatever else he can afford. He must fulfill the vow he has made, according to the law of the Nazirite.'"

[16 NIV] "`If a man strikes someone with an iron object so that he dies, he is a murderer; the murderer shall be put to death.

[21 NIV] or if in hostility he hits him with his fist so that he dies, that person shall be put to death; he is a murderer. The avenger of blood shall put the murderer to death when he meets him.
[21 KJV] Or in enmity smite him with his hand, that he die: he that smote him shall surely be put to death; for he is a murderer: the revenger of blood shall slay the murderer, when he meeteth him.

[22 KJV] But if he thrust him suddenly without enmity, or have cast upon him any thing without laying of wait,

[24 NIV] the assembly must judge between him and the avenger of blood according to these regulations.

[25 KJV] And the congregation shall deliver the slayer out of the hand of the revenger of blood, and the congregation shall restore him to the city of his refuge, whither he was fled: and he shall abide in it unto the death of the high priest, which was anointed with the holy oil.
[26 NIV] "`But if the accused ever goes outside the limits of the city of refuge to which he has fled
[26 KJV] But if the slayer shall at any time come without the border of the city of his refuge, whither he was fled;
[27 NIV] and the avenger of blood finds him outside the city, the avenger of blood may kill the accused without being guilty of murder.
[27 KJV] And the revenger of blood find him without the borders of the city of his refuge, and the revenger of blood kill the slayer; he shall not be guilty of blood:
[28 NIV] The accused must stay in his city of refuge until the death of the high priest; only after the death of the high priest may he return to his own property.
[28 KJV] Because he should have remained in the city of his refuge until the death of the high priest: but after the death of the high priest the slayer shall return into the land of his possession.
[29 NIV] "`These are to be legal requirements for you throughout the generations to come, wherever you live.
[29 KJV] So these things shall be for a statute of judgment unto you throughout your generations in all your dwellings.
[30 NIV] "`Anyone who kills a person is to be put to death as a murderer only on the testimony of witnesses. But no one is to be put to death on the testimony of only one witness.
[30 KJV] Whoso killeth any person, the murderer shall be put to death by the mouth of witnesses: but one witness shall not testify against any person to cause him to die.
[31 NIV] "`Do not accept a ransom for the life of a murderer, who deserves to die. He must surely be put to death.
[31 KJV] Moreover ye shall take no satisfaction for the life of a murderer, which is guilty of death: but he shall be surely put to death.
[32 NIV] "`Do not accept a ransom for anyone who has fled to a city of refuge and so allow him to go back and live on his own land before the death of the high priest.
[32 KJV] And ye shall take no satisfaction for him that is fled to the city of his refuge, that he should come again to dwell in the land, until the death of the priest.
[33 NIV] "`Do not pollute the land where you are. Bloodshed pollutes the land, and atonement cannot be made for the land on which blood has been shed, except by the blood of the one who shed it.
[33 KJV] So ye shall not pollute the land wherein ye are: for blood it defileth the land: and the land cannot be cleansed of the blood that is shed therein, but by the blood of him that shed it.
[34 NIV] Do not defile the land where you live and where I dwell, for I, the LORD, dwell among the Israelites.'"
[34 KJV] Defile not therefore the land which ye shall inhabit, wherein I dwell: for I the LORD dwell among the children of Israel.

Chapter 36

[1 NIV] The family heads of the clan of Gilead son of Makir, the son of Manasseh, who were from the clans of the descendants of Joseph, came and spoke before Moses and the leaders, the heads of the Israelite families.
[1 KJV] And the chief fathers of the families of the children of Gilead, the son of Machir, the son of Manasseh, of the families of the sons of Joseph, came near, and spake before Moses, and before the princes, the chief fathers of the children of Israel:
[2 NIV] They said, "When the LORD commanded my lord to give the land as an inheritance to the Israelites by lot, he ordered you to give the inheritance of our brother Zelophehad to his daughters.
[2 KJV] And they said, The LORD commanded my lord to give the land for an inheritance by lot to the children of Israel: and my lord was commanded by the LORD to give the inheritance of Zelophehad our brother unto his daughters.
[3 NIV] Now suppose they marry men from other Israelite tribes; then their inheritance will be taken from our ancestral inheritance and added to that of the tribe they marry into. And so part of the inheritance allotted to us will be taken away.
[3 KJV] And if they be married to any of the sons of the other tribes of the children of Israel, then shall their inheritance be taken from the inheritance of our fathers, and shall be put to the inheritance of the tribe whereunto they are received: so shall it be taken from the lot of our inheritance.
[4 NIV] When the Year of Jubilee for the Israelites comes, their inheritance will be added to that of the tribe into which they marry, and their property will be taken from the tribal inheritance of our forefathers."
[4 KJV] And when the jubile of the children of Israel shall be, then shall their inheritance be put unto the inheritance of the tribe whereunto they are received: so shall their inheritance be taken away from the inheritance of the tribe of our fathers.
[5 NIV] Then at the LORD's command Moses gave this order to the Israelites: "What the tribe of the descendants of Joseph is saying is right.
[5 KJV] And Moses commanded the children of Israel according to the word of the LORD, saying, The tribe of the sons of Joseph hath said well.
[6 NIV] This is what the LORD commands for Zelophehad's daughters: They may marry anyone they please as long as they marry within the tribal clan of their father.
[6 KJV] This is the thing which the LORD doth command concerning the daughters of Zelophehad, saying, Let them marry to whom they think best; only to the family of the tribe of their father shall they marry.
[7 NIV] No inheritance in Israel is to pass from tribe to tribe, for every Israelite shall keep the tribal land inherited from his forefathers.
[7 KJV] So shall not the inheritance of the children of Israel remove from tribe to tribe: for every one of the children of Israel shall keep himself to the inheritance of the tribe of his fathers.
[8 NIV] Every daughter who inherits land in any Israelite tribe must marry someone in her father's tribal clan, so that every Israelite will possess the inheritance of his fathers.
[8 KJV] And every daughter, that possesseth an inheritance in any tribe of the children of Israel, shall be wife unto one of the family of the tribe of her father, that the children of Israel may enjoy every man the inheritance of his fathers.
[9 NIV] No inheritance may pass from tribe to tribe, for each Israelite tribe is to keep the land it inherits."
[9 KJV] Neither shall the inheritance remove from one tribe to another tribe; but every one of the tribes of the children of Israel shall keep himself to his own inheritance.
[10 NIV] So Zelophehad's daughters did as the LORD commanded Moses.
[10 KJV] Even as the LORD commanded Moses, so did the daughters of Zelophehad:
[11 NIV] Zelophehad's daughters--Mahlah, Tirzah, Hoglah, Milcah and Noah--married their cousins on their father's side.
[11 KJV] For Mahlah, Tirzah, and Hoglah, and Milcah, and Noah, the daughters of Zelophehad, were married unto their father's brothers' sons:
[12 NIV] They married within the clans of the descendants of Manasseh son of Joseph, and their inheritance remained in their father's clan and tribe.
[12 KJV] And they were married into the families of the sons of Manasseh the son of Joseph, and their inheritance remained in the tribe of the family of their father.
